        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer409800028" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9588097958595945314">I can't believe it's over, no, no I can't. The emotional roller coaster I search for in every book came through with shuddering effect throughout this series - from elation, to abject fear, absolute sorrow, knuckle biting suspense, to sobs of "Why?! Why, oh why!" all the way to the sated peace that I've yet to find in so many other promising stories. <br/><br/>I don't say this lightly, but the Elemental Mysteries is going to linger in my head for a very, very long time. <br/><br/>This book in particular - I fell in</span>
  <span id="freeText9588097958595945314" style="display:none">I can't believe it's over, no, no I can't. The emotional roller coaster I search for in every book came through with shuddering effect throughout this series - from elation, to abject fear, absolute sorrow, knuckle biting suspense, to sobs of "Why?! Why, oh why!" all the way to the sated peace that I've yet to find in so many other promising stories. <br /><br />I don't say this lightly, but the Elemental Mysteries is going to linger in my head for a very, very long time. <br /><br />This book in particular - I fell in love all over again with the deep connection between Beatrice and Gio, a connection that went beyond simple "love", "trust" and "contentment".<br /><br />I would absolutely go crazy if a spin-off series was written about Ben. Like, batshit crazy. <br /><br />I was intrigued by the introduction of Ziri, Arosh, Kato and Saba but I felt that their presence was too fleeting - too convenient to tie up loose ends. Perhaps a short story about Saba? That would quell my curiosity for who Elizabeth Hunter introduces as "the first of their kind".<br /><br />The final scene with Gio and Lorenzo really put me at peace. It happened exactly how I imagined, how I thought Gio would handle it and Beatrice was absolutely on point. I know that a book is well written when the characterization of each persona echoes exactly in my head - there is no OOC incidences and I'm not sitting here thinking its a load of garbage. <br /><br />I can't blab enough praise for this series! Unconditional 5/5 stars. <br /></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16252756141591021006">A superb conclusion to a 5 star series!<br/>A Fall of Water, the fourth and final book of Elizabeth Hunter’s Elemental Mysteries series starts off with the characters dealing with the aftermath of the events in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13414389.The_Force_of_Wind__Elemental_Mysteries__3_' title='The Force of Wind (Elemental Mysteries #3) by Elizabeth Hunter' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Force of Wind</a>. After regrouping and some seclusion time for B, the team sets out to find the vampire supporting Lorenzo as well as Lorenzo himself. The conclusion to Beatrice & Gio’s story does not falter. The story never feels rushed or contrived as mysteries are solved, loose ends wrappe</span>
  <span id="freeText16252756141591021006" style="display:none">A superb conclusion to a 5 star series!<br />A Fall of Water, the fourth and final book of Elizabeth Hunter’s Elemental Mysteries series starts off with the characters dealing with the aftermath of the events in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13414389.The_Force_of_Wind__Elemental_Mysteries__3_" title="The Force of Wind (Elemental Mysteries #3) by Elizabeth Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">The Force of Wind</a>. After regrouping and some seclusion time for B, the team sets out to find the vampire supporting Lorenzo as well as Lorenzo himself. The conclusion to Beatrice &amp; Gio’s story does not falter. The story never feels rushed or contrived as mysteries are solved, loose ends wrapped up or a certain character’s motivation revealed.<br /><br />At the end of the last book I decided that I needed an action figure of Beatrice, A Fall of Water did not change that, but now I must have a Tenzin figure as well. The action scenes featuring the two women were incredible and heart stopping. As it was the last book in the series (not counting the highly anticipated spin off books set in the same universe) I wasn’t positive that Ms. Hunter wouldn’t kill off some of her heroes before the end of the story.<br /><br />The books are also a fantastic value, for less than $15 you can purchase all 4 books in the series. Lots of bang for your buck, you won’t be disappointed. I look forward to reading more about her vampires in Carwyn’s book.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10794021621023679005">What can I say I haven't already said in my previous reviews regarding this series - it is one of the best I have ever read and one I WILL read again.<br/><br/>In book four - the finale one in this series - Gio and B have to go through another set of dangerous problems , till they are finally able to solve the mystery.   <span id="freeText10794021621023679005" style="display:none">What can I say I haven't already said in my previous reviews regarding this series - it is one of the best I have ever read and one I WILL read again.<br /><br />In book four - the finale one in this series - Gio and B have to go through another set of dangerous problems , till they are finally able to solve the mystery. The reading, was as always, so engaging and captivating, that I had to pace myself to slow down, because I did not want to be done too soon.<br /><br />The enemies are getting more volatile, the friends are getting stronger, the love between the hero and the heroine is growing . <br /><br />This book is another notch up the previous ones ( if that is even possible - and it seemed , it was ). I truly appreciate Ms Hunters writing and I hope , she will continue to write ( esp. the many stories left in the world of Elements ) I can wait , Ms Hunter, but I would love to read, Carwyns, Tenzins ,Bens and all the other characters in the world you created.</span>

<div id="review_342987425" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/342987425" />
    <a title="Michelle(Chelle) aka Nightshade - Cake Whisperer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3731017-michelle-chelle-aka-nightshade---cake-whisperer"><img alt="Michelle(Chelle) aka Nightshade - Cake Whisperer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1308243560p2/3731017.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/342987425?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle(Chelle) aka Nightshade - Cake Whisperer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle(Chelle) aka Nightshade - Cake Whisperer" href="/user/show/3731017-michelle-chelle-aka-nightshade---cake-whisperer">Michelle(Chelle) aka Nightshade - Cake Whisperer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">All PNR readers that like a well written love story</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer342987425" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9059486508434408552">Ms Hunter has done it again. This last book in the Elemental Mysteries series has everything.....Romance, Action, Humor, Great Characters, History.....What a wonderful read. Book 4 reunites us with Bea & Gio, who IMO are such a sweet, sexy couple. Just having the two of them on the page together is steamy....must be the fire/water combination. All of our favorite supporting characters are back: Carwyn, Tenzin, Ben, Dez & Matt. Some new characters have been added and I will admit to getting attac</span>
  <span id="freeText9059486508434408552" style="display:none">Ms Hunter has done it again. This last book in the Elemental Mysteries series has everything.....Romance, Action, Humor, Great Characters, History.....What a wonderful read. Book 4 reunites us with Bea &amp; Gio, who IMO are such a sweet, sexy couple. Just having the two of them on the page together is steamy....must be the fire/water combination. All of our favorite supporting characters are back: Carwyn, Tenzin, Ben, Dez &amp; Matt. Some new characters have been added and I will admit to getting attached to most of them as well. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I really liked Donatella and was really sad when she died in the final battle <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.The storyline that was begun in A Hidden Fire comes to an excellent, satisfying conclusion. This is a well written series that has a lot of meat to the story. I am looking forward to reading more on the side characters.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9059486508434408552" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1973826967" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1973826967" />
    <a title="Rachmi " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3047938-rachmi"><img alt="Rachmi " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1358842498p2/3047938.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1973826967?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachmi " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachmi " href="/user/show/3047938-rachmi">Rachmi </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781476237725" href="/book/show/21640825-a-fall-of-water">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3047938-rachmi?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3047938-rachmi?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3047938-rachmi?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1973826967" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16407338363263191463">As the last book, it was a bit let down. I liked the series all right but it didn't wow me either while I kept hoping that each book will be better than the previous. But with the resemble of Twilight series, it was quite hard for me to love it. Not that I'm against Twilight, though I'm not a fan either. But I was wishing that it won't be that similar, as I was interested in Giovanni and Beatrice’s story.<br/> <br/>It was good it has its own story here, the resemble wasn't that prominent like in the first</span>
  <span id="freeText16407338363263191463" style="display:none">As the last book, it was a bit let down. I liked the series all right but it didn't wow me either while I kept hoping that each book will be better than the previous. But with the resemble of Twilight series, it was quite hard for me to love it. Not that I'm against Twilight, though I'm not a fan either. But I was wishing that it won't be that similar, as I was interested in Giovanni and Beatrice’s story.<br /> <br />It was good it has its own story here, the resemble wasn't that prominent like in the first three books. I don't know if it's because it's the last book, or because it's been months since I read book 3 or because I don't exactly have any hope it won't have similarity to Twilight series anymore, either way I tried to enjoy it as it is and kept away the Twilight series from my mind while reading this last Giovanni and Beatrice’s journey. <br /><br />But the thing is it was pretty boring. Just like in previous books, the story is often jump to months and only fill in by one description from one POV. When this is the last book, I thought it will have action with fast-paced. But I found quite the opposite. And when Giovanni and Beatrice’s fill the time gap they weren't that interesting. Not to mention that they mostly talk and rarely take action. I know that they building the connection, strategizing and all that but for the life of me I just want them to take action so that I can finish the story. <br /><br />I still have things I enjoyed though. Still like Tenzin and Benjamin and Giovanni and Beatrice’s relationship with them and other characters. And the writing is nice too. So I think it's an okay reading, though not so much as a series. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16407338363263191463" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TerWr0O+6FSIm0fyT/PVFUNuWVRzr0pZ6iKh8R3Za+cLAK22A4jWNX32WxUrVRT/VrOs+6+2cpHgsD/unS3h/g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('uMmlA9fXYwAvBGFeSf4T2TeHdeZeGRAfZtlvNZN1akD+I94al+FdYdppfbktWNIzIlqASYIAKNdsS/EqE4HgWQ==')})
  }
